# USAA
USA_foreign_policy_category = {

	TNO_jamaica_guerrilla_attack = {
		priority = 10
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_ignite_civil_war
		activation = {
			has_country_flag = USA_jamaica_crisis_guerrillas
		}
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}

		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 7

		timeout_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = TNO_jamaica_crisis_guerillas_done
			clr_country_flag = USA_jamaica_crisis_guerrillas
		}
	}

	TNO_jamaica_intensify_OFN_propaganda = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_propaganda

		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_jamaican_referendum_selected = yes
		}
		available = {
			TNO_US_interventions_not_blocked = yes
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}

		cost = 10

		days_remove = 7
		fire_only_once = no
		days_re_enable = 0

		complete_effect = {
			TNO_decrease_jamaica_indep_chance_low = yes
			TNO_increase_us_intervention_low = yes
		}
	}

	TNO_jamaica_court_JLP_leaders = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_political_discourse
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_jamaican_referendum_selected = yes
			#WIN = { check_variable = { WIN_foreign_intervention > 40 } }
		}
		available = {
			TNO_US_interventions_not_blocked = yes
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}

		custom_cost_trigger = { check_variable = { GDP > 0 } }
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_50_million

		days_remove = 14
		fire_only_once = no
		days_re_enable = 0

		complete_effect = {
			TNO_decrease_jamaica_indep_daily_tick_low = yes
			TNO_increase_us_intervention_low = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = TNO_jamaica_court_JLP_leaders_cost
			hidden_effect = {
				set_temp_variable = { removed_from_reserves = money_reserves }
				clamp_temp_variable = { var = removed_from_reserves min = 0 max = 0.05 }
				set_temp_variable = { to_add_to_debt = 0.05 }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { to_add_to_debt = removed_from_reserves }
				add_to_variable = { national_debt = to_add_to_debt }
			}
		}
	}

	TNO_jamaica_blackmail_independence_activists = {
		icon = GFX_decision_document_cancel
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_jamaican_referendum_selected = yes
			#WIN = { check_variable = { WIN_foreign_intervention > 75 } }
		}
		available = {
			TNO_US_interventions_not_blocked = yes
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				check_variable = { WIN.WIN_us_intervention > 75 }
			}
		}

		cost = 35

		days_remove = 21
		fire_only_once = no
		days_re_enable = 0

		complete_effect = {
			TNO_decrease_jamaica_indep_chance_med = yes
			TNO_increase_us_intervention_high = yes
		}
	}




	TNO_jamaica_postpone_referendum = {
		icon = GFX_decision_clock
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_jamaican_referendum_selected = yes
		}
		available = {
			TNO_foreign_intervention_medium_us = yes

			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = TNO_jamaica_postpone_referendum_trigger
				check_variable = { WIN.WIN_referendum_times_delayed < 3 }
			}
			TNO_US_interventions_not_blocked = yes
		}
		days_remove = 7
		fire_only_once = no

		cost = 15

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				check_variable = { WIN.WIN_referendum_times_delayed > 0 }
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			TNO_increase_jamaica_indep_daily_tick_low = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = TNO_jamaica_postpone_referendum_effect

			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { WIN.WIN_referendum_times_delayed = 0 } }
				WIN = { set_country_flag = TNO_WIN_delay_happening }
				} else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { WIN.WIN_referendum_times_delayed = 1 } }
				WIN = { set_country_flag = TNO_WIN_delay_happening_2 }
				} else = {
				WIN = { set_country_flag = TNO_WIN_delay_happening_3 }
			}


			hidden_effect = {
				WIN = {
					add_to_variable = { WIN_referendum_days_left = 7 }
					add_to_variable = { WIN_referendum_days_max = 7 }
					add_to_variable = { WIN_referendum_times_delayed = 1 }


					# Recompute clock
					set_variable = { WIN_referendum_fill = 100 }
					multiply_variable = { WIN_referendum_fill = WIN_referendum_days_left }
					divide_variable = { WIN_referendum_fill = WIN_referendum_days_max }
				}

			}
		}
	}


	TNO_jamaica_investigate_interference = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_investigate
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_jamaican_referendum_selected = yes
		}
		available = {
			TNO_foreign_intervention_high_us = yes
			TNO_US_interventions_not_blocked = yes
		}
		days_remove = 14
		fire_only_once = no
		days_re_enable = 30

		cost = 35

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 50
		}

		complete_effect = {
			WIN = { set_country_flag = TNO_WIN_investigation_happening }
		}
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = TNO_jamaica_investigate_interference_effect
			WIN = { clr_country_flag = TNO_WIN_investigation_happening }

			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { TNO_foreign_intervention_high_us = yes }
					TNO_decrease_jamaica_indep_chance_med = yes
					TNO_decrease_jamaica_indep_daily_tick_low = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	TNO_jamaica_dial_back_rhetoric = {
		icon = GFX_decision_propaganda_off
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_jamaican_referendum_selected = yes
		}
		available = {

			TNO_US_interventions_not_blocked = yes
			TNO_US_intervention_medium_us = yes
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 500
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				check_variable = { WIN.WIN_us_intervention < 80 }
			}
		}

		days_remove = 14
		fire_only_once = no
		days_re_enable = 0
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_jamaica_crisis_intervention_blocked
			TNO_increase_jamaica_indep_chance_med = yes
			TNO_decrease_us_intervention_high = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = TNO_jamaica_dial_back_rhetoric_effect
		}
		remove_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = USA_jamaica_crisis_intervention_blocked
		}
	}
}

USA_foreign_policy_category = {
	TNO_jamaica_crisis_restoring_order = {
		priority = 10
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_propaganda
		activation = {
			check_variable = { WIN.WIN_fervor < 10.1 }
			WIN = { has_country_flag = Jamaica_Crisis_Unresolved }
		}
		available = {
			TNO_jamaica_crisis_fervor_not_low = yes
		}

		is_good = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 7
		days_remove = 1

		timeout_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = TNO_jamaica_crisis_restoring_order_effect
			hidden_effect = {
				TNO_end_jamaica_crisis_calmed = yes
			}
		}
	}
	TNO_jamaica_crisis_losing_control = {
		priority = 10
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_civil_support
		activation = {

			WIN = { has_country_flag = Jamaica_Crisis_Unresolved }
		}
		available = {

		}

		days_remove = 1

			custom_effect_tooltip = TNO_jamaica_crisis_losing_control_effect
			hidden_effect = {
				TNO_end_jamaica_crisis_coup = yes
			}
		}
	}


	TNO_jamaica_crisis_approach_the_students = {
		icon = GFX_decision_handshake

		days_re_enable = 0

				check_variable = { WIN.WIN_violence > 50 }

		complete_effect = {
			TNO_decrease_fervor_low_violence_sensitive = yes
		}
	}
	TNO_jamaica_crisis_parley_jlp = {

		days_re_enable = 0

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 25

				check_variable = { WIN.WIN_violence < 25 }
			}
		}

		cost = 25

		complete_effect = {
			TNO_decrease_crisis_violence_low = yes
		}
	}
	TNO_jamaica_crisis_arrest_troublemakers = {
		icon = GFX_decision_arrest

		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_jamaican_crisis_selected = yes
			WIN = { has_country_flag = Jamaica_Crisis_Unresolved }
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					check_variable = { WIN.WIN_violence < 50 }
					check_variable = { WIN.WIN_fervor > 75 }

				NOT = { has_country_flag = WAC_active_shipment }
			}
		}

		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_wac_selected = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = WAC_large_shipments_enabled }
			OR = {
				is_ai = yes
				has_country_flag = WAC_ground_vehicles_shipments_visible
			}
		}

		custom_cost_trigger = {
			has_political_power > 14
			command_power > 4
		}
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_5_cp_15_pp

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = { global.WAC_escalation > 4 }
			}
		}

		target_array = global.west_african_nations
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = FFR
					AND = {
						NOT = {
							country_exists = FFR
							has_global_flag = WAC_scenario_2
						}
						is_in_faction_with = WOL
					}
				}
			}
		}

		days_remove = 21
		days_re_enable = 30
		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 add_political_power = -15 }
			set_country_flag = WAC_active_shipment
		}
		remove_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = WAC_active_shipment
			send_equipment = {
				type = motorized_equipment_2
				amount = 200
				target = FROM
			}
			send_equipment = {
				type = APC_equipment_2
				amount = 80
				target = FROM
			}
			send_equipment = {
				type = MBT_equipment_2
				amount = 50
				target = FROM
			}
			send_equipment = {
				type = IFV_equipment_2
				amount = 30
				target = FROM
			}
		}

	JAP_bombing_runs_WA = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_bombing
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_wac_selected = yes
			has_country_flag = JAP_In_The_WAC_WAR
		}

		days_re_enable = 120
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 14.99 }
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_15_cp
		days_remove = 90

		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -15 }
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision JAP_bombing_runs"
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = FFR }
				every_country = {
					limit = { is_in_faction_with = FFR }
					add_timed_idea = {
						idea = JAP_Plane_Bombing
						days = 90
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = WAC_scenario_1
						has_global_flag = WAC_scenario_3
					}
					NOT = { country_exists = FFR }
					country_exists = WOL
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = { is_in_faction_with = WOL }

					add_timed_idea = {
						idea = JAP_Plane_Bombing
						days = 90
					}
				}				
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = WAC_scenario_2 }

			custom_effect_tooltip = BOR_OC_baath_unhappy_tt
			add_to_variable = { BOR_OC_participation = -5 }
			clamp_variable = { var = BOR_OC_participation min = 0 max = 100 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = econ_increase_money_reserves
			add_to_variable = { money_reserves = 0.5 } #already converted to billion
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
		}
	}

## Boring man (Bormann)
GER_foreign_policy_category = {
	GER_Bormann_OC_send_weapons = {
		icon = GFX_decision_black_market_infantry_purchase
		available = {
			has_equipment = { infantry_equipment > 599 }
			has_equipment = { anti_tank_equipment > 349 }
			has_equipment = { support_equipment > 399 }
		}
		targets = { EGB SYR BIR NYM OMB GUL PAL SDS }
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				exists = yes
				has_war = yes
				if = {
					limit = { tag = GUL }
					has_government = social_democracy
				}
				if = {
					limit = { tag = PAL }
					OR = {
						has_government = communist
						has_government = ultranationalism
					}
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			FROM = {
				exists = yes
				has_war = yes
			}
			TNO_fopo_baathism_support_selected = yes
		}

		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 4 }
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_5_cp
		days_remove = 3
		days_re_enable = 21

		highlight_states = {
			is_owned_and_controlled_by = FROM
			is_capital = yes
		}
		on_map_mode = map_only

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision GER_Bormann_OC_send_weapons"
			hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 }
		}
		remove_effect = {
			send_equipment = {
				type = infantry_equipment
				amount = 600
				target = FROM
			}
			send_equipment = {
				type = anti_tank_equipment
				amount = 350
				target = FROM
			}
			send_equipment = {
				type = support_equipment
				amount = 400
				target = FROM
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				BOR_OC_participation = 2.5
				tooltip = BOR_OC_add_participation
			}
			clamp_variable = { var = BOR_OC_participation min = 0 max = 100 }
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
		}
	}

USA_foreign_policy_category = {

	USA_OC_increase_commitment = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
		visible = {
			tag = USA
			TNO_fopo_baathism_support_selected = yes
			TNO_volunteer_cap_less_5 = yes
			check_variable = {
				USA_OC_volunteer_sent < 3
			}
		}

		cost = 50
		days_re_enable = 21

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_OC_increase_commitment"
			add_command_power = 25

			for_each_scope_loop  = {
				array = global.OIL_supported_by_USA

				USA = {
					set_temp_variable = { target = PREV }
					TNO_increase_volunteer_cap_1 = yes
				}
			}

			add_to_variable = {
				USA_OC_volunteer_sent = 1 
			}

			custom_effect_tooltip = OIL_USA_increase_volunteers_1

			
			add_to_variable = {
				USA_OC_participation = 8
				tooltip = BOR_OC_add_participation
			}
			clamp_variable = { var = USA_OC_participation min = 0 max = 100 }
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
		}
	}

	USA_OC_bomb_someone = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_bombing
		targets = { EGY RPS AZA OMI OMA IRP IRQ YEM }
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				exists = yes
				has_war = yes
				is_in_array = {
					array = global.OIL_supported_by_USA
					value = THIS
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			FROM = {
				exists = yes
				has_war = yes
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = USA_OC_being_bombed
				}
			}
			TNO_fopo_baathism_support_selected = yes
		}

		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 14.99 }
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_15_cp
		days_remove = 90
		days_re_enable = 21

		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view
		highlight_states = {
			is_controlled_by = FROM
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_OC_bomb_someone"
			hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -15 }
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { has_war_with = FROM }
				add_ideas = USA_OC_bombing_runs
				set_country_flag = USA_OC_being_bombed
				TNO_worsen_poverty_high = yes
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				USA_OC_participation = 5
				tooltip = BOR_OC_add_participation
			}
			clamp_variable = { var = USA_OC_participation min = 0 max = 100 }
		}
		remove_effect = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_OC_being_bombed }
				remove_ideas = USA_OC_bombing_runs
				clr_country_flag = USA_OC_being_bombed
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
		}

			acclimatization_hot_climate_gain_factor = 0.2
			heat_attrition_factor = -0.2
			recon_factor = 0.1
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision JAP_OC_heat_of_the_desert"
			hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -10 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_spending_amount = 0.025 }
			econ_spend_money_once_effect_raw_money = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
		}
	}
}

					}

			}
		}

	}

GER_foreign_policy_category = {
	GER_Bormann_SAF_war_report = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_assault
		activation = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = GER_SAW_intervention
					has_global_flag = south_african_war
					has_global_flag = german_civil_war_bormannvic
				}
				has_country_flag = BOR_DBG_SAF_war
			}
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = SAF_WAR_OVER
				has_completed_focus = BOR_ende_ohne_sieg
			}
		}
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = SAF_WAR_OVER
					has_completed_focus = BOR_ende_ohne_sieg
					NOT = { has_global_flag = south_african_war }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = GER_SAW_intervention }
				}
			}
		}

		is_good = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 14

# Speer
GER_foreign_policy_category = {
	SGR_SAW_war_report = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_assault

		activation = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				has_global_flag = german_civil_war_speervic
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = SGR_natsoc_collapse
					has_completed_focus = GER_bear_no_responsibility
					has_global_flag = SAF_WAR_OVER
					NOT = { has_global_flag = south_african_war }
				}
			}
		}

		is_good = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 28

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Mission SGR_SAW_war_report"
			SGR_SAW_protest_growth = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						NOT = {has_completed_focus = GER_finish_what_we_started}
						NOT = {has_global_flag = south_african_war}
					}
				}
				activate_mission = SGR_SAW_war_report
			}
		}
	}

	SGR_SAW_war_effort_failure = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_assault

		activation = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = SGR_SAW_war_failure_tt
				hidden_trigger = {
					NOT = {check_variable = {SGR_SAW_civilian_protest < 90}}
					has_global_flag = german_civil_war_speervic
					NOT = {has_global_flag = SGR_natsoc_collapse}
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = south_african_war
						has_country_flag = SGR_SAF_debug
					}
				}
			}

		}

		ai_will_do = {

		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { 
			command_power > 14.99
		 }
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_15_cp
		days_remove = 90

			hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -15 }
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_bombing_runs"
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = US_aid_gazaland_simango }
				if = { #Check for whether Simango was supported and 2 countries need to be hit
					limit = { country_exists = GAZ } #Don't hit annexed countries
					GAZ = {
						add_timed_idea = {
							idea = USA_Plane_Bombing
							days = 90
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { country_exists = GZO }
					GZO = {
						add_timed_idea = {
							idea = USA_Plane_Bombing
							days = 90
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {

			}
		}

	USA_USFIP_recon_timeout = {
		icon = GFX_decision_clock
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_philippines_war_selected = yes
		}
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}
		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 180
		selectable_mission = no
		timeout_effect = {
		    if = { 
		        limit = {
			        has_game_rule = {
				        rule = UPH_ideology
				        option = UPH_IDEOLOGY_FAILED_RECONSTRUCTION
			        }
		        }
	            set_variable = { PHI_reconstruction_var = 0 }
	        }
	        else_if = { 
		        limit = {
			        has_game_rule = {
				        rule = UPH_ideology
				        option = UPH_IDEOLOGY_RUMULO
			        }
		        }
	            set_variable = { PHI_reconstruction_var = 100 }
	            set_country_flag = USA_PHI_delegitimized_leyte
	        }
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
					check_variable = { PHI_reconstruction_var = 100 }
				}
				PHI_reconstruction_complete = yes
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = USA_USFIP_recon_timeout_tt
				hidden_effect = { country_event = PHI_Blitz.22 }
				TNO_fopo_remove_philippines_reconstruction_tab = yes
			}
		}
	}

		        limit = {
			        has_game_rule = {
				        rule = SPH_coalition_path
				        option = SPH_COALITION_PATH_FAILED_RECONSTRUCTION
			        }
		        }
	            set_variable = { PHI_reconstruction_var = 0 }
	        }
	        else_if = { 
		        limit = {
		            OR = {
			            has_game_rule = {
				            rule = SPH_coalition_path
				            option = SPH_COALITION_PATH_TARUC
			            }
			            has_game_rule = {
				            rule = SPH_coalition_path
				            option = SPH_COALITION_PATH_TANADA
			            }
		            }
		        }
	            set_variable = { PHI_reconstruction_var = 100 }
	        }
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
					check_variable = { PHI_reconstruction_var = 100 }
				}
				PHI_reconstruction_complete = yes
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = USA_SPH_recon_timeout_tt
				hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = PHI_Blitz.200 days = 30 } }
				TNO_fopo_remove_philippines_reconstruction_tab = yes	
			}
		}
	}
}

	JAP_PHI_recon_timeout = {
		icon = GFX_decision_clock
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_philippines_war_selected = yes
		}
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}
		activation = {

		}
		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 180
		selectable_mission = no

		    if = { 
		        limit = {
			        has_game_rule = {
				        rule = PHI_ideology
				        option = PHI_IDEOLOGY_FAILED_RECONSTRUCTION
			        }
		        }
	            set_variable = { PHI_reconstruction_var = 0 }
	        }
	        else_if = { 
		        limit = {
		            OR = {
			            has_game_rule = {
				            rule = PHI_ideology
				            option = PHI_IDEOLOGY_PAREDES
			            }
			            has_game_rule = {
				            rule = PHI_ideology
				            option = PHI_IDEOLOGY_RECTO
			            }
			            has_game_rule = {
				            rule = PHI_ideology
				            option = PHI_IDEOLOGY_OSMENA
			            }
		            }
		        }
	            set_variable = { PHI_reconstruction_var = 100 }
	        }
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
					check_variable = { PHI_reconstruction_var = 100 }
				}
				PHI_reconstruction_complete = yes
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = JAP_PHI_recon_timeout_tt
				hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = PHI_Blitz.24 days = 1 } }
				TNO_fopo_remove_philippines_reconstruction_tab = yes
			}
		}
	}

		is_good = yes

		fire_only_once = no

		activation = {
			has_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Activated
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Pulled_Out }
		}

		timeout_effect = {

			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Discontent_Fall_Low
			randomize_temp_variable = {
				var = SAF_relief
				distribution = uniform
				min = 6
				max = 10
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { USA_SAF_WAR_Discontent = SAF_relief }
		}
	}

	USA_SAF_Can_Pull_Out = {
		icon = GFX_decision_clock
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Pulled_Out }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_can_pull_out_mandates }
			}
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 400

		fire_only_once = yes

		activation = {
			has_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Activated
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Pulled_Out }
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				ZZZ = {
					country_event = {
						id = SAFWAR.11111
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
